class="flex items-center gap-2 justify-between font-medium text-stone-900 py-1 dark:text-white mb-1 not-first:mt-4">Core Concepts</p><ul><li><div class="ms-2"><details class="group not-first:mt-4" class="ms-2"><p class="flex items-center gap-2 justify-between font-medium text-stone-900 py-1 dark:text-white mb-1 not-first:mt-4">Reference</p><ul><li><a class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md flex items-center transition-colors relative hover:text-stone-900 dark:hover:text-stone-200" href="/docs/react/reference/faq"><span class="">FAQs</span></a></li><li><a class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md flex items-center transition-colors relative hover:text-stone-900 dark:hover:text-stone-200" href="/docs/react/reference/performance"><span class="">Performance tips</span></a></li><li><div class="ms-2"><details class="group not-first:mt-4" open=""><summary class="list-none"><div class="flex items-center gap-2 justify-between font-medium text-stone-900 py-1 dark:text-white mb-1 not-first:mt-4"><span class="flex-1">Design patterns</span><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down rounded-xs text-stone-700 dark:text-stone-100 group-open:rotate-180 transition-transform group-hover:text-stone-500 text-stone-400 dark:text-stone-600" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m6 9 6 6 6-6"></path></svg></div></summary><ul><li><a class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md flex items-center transition-colors relative hover:text-stone-900 dark:hover:text-stone-200" href="/docs/react/reference/design-patterns/form"><span class="">Forms</span></a></li><li><a class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md flex items-center transition-colors relative hover:text-stone-900 dark:hover:text-stone-200" href="/docs/react/reference/design-patterns/organization"><span class="">Organization/Team</span></a></li><li><a class="py-1 px-2 group rounded-md flex items-center transition-colors relative hover:text-stone-900 dark:hover:text-stone-200" href="/docs/react/reference/design-patterns/history-patterns"><span class="">History Patterns</span></a></li></ul></details></div></li></ul></div></li></ul><div aria-hidden="true" class="h-12 right-0 sticky bottom-0 left-0 bg-linear-to-t from-white  to-transparent dark:from-stone-950 hidden md:block"></div></div></div></div><div class="md:col-span-8 lg:col-span-9 flex gap-12"><div class="w-full" data-pagefind-body="true" data-pagefind-meta="framework: react"><div class="overflow-hidden pb-8 pt-[calc(61px+2rem)] md:pt-8 md:max-w-3xl mx-auto prose dark:prose-invert dark:prose-code:bg-stone-900"><h1 id="defining-schemas-covalues">Defining schemas: CoValues</h1>
<p><strong>CoValues (&quot;Collaborative Values&quot;) are the core abstraction of Jazz.</strong> They&#x27;re your bread-and-butter datastructures that you use to represent everything in your app.</p>
<p>As their name suggests, CoValues are inherently collaborative, meaning <strong>multiple users and devices can edit them at the same time.</strong></p>
<p><strong>Think of CoValues as &quot;super-fast Git for lots of tiny data.&quot;</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>CoValues keep their full edit histories, from which they derive their &quot;current state&quot;.</li>
<li>The fact that this happens in an eventually-consistent way makes them <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Conflict-free_replicated_data_type">CRDTs</a>.</li>
<li>Having the full history also means that you often don&#x27;t need explicit timestamps and author info - you get this for free as part of a CoValue&#x27;s <a href="/docs/react/key-features/history">edit metadata</a>.</li>
</ul>
<p>CoValues model JSON with CoMaps and CoLists, but also offer CoFeeds for simple per-user value feeds, and let you represent binary data with FileStreams.</p>
<h2 id="start-your-app-with-a-schema" class="group"><a href="#start-your-app-with-a-schema" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Start your app with a schema</span></h2>
<p>Fundamentally, CoValues are as dynamic and flexible as JSON, but in Jazz you use them by defining fixed schemas to describe the shape of data in your app.</p>
<p>This helps correctness and development speed, but is particularly important...</p>
<ul>
<li>when you evolve your app and need migrations</li>
<li>when different clients and server workers collaborate on CoValues and need to make compatible changes</li>
</ul>
<p>Thinking about the shape of your data is also a great first step to model your app.</p>
<p>Even before you know the details of how your app will work, you&#x27;ll probably know which kinds of objects it will deal with, and how they relate to each other.</p>
<p>In Jazz, you define schemas using <code>co</code> for CoValues and <code>z</code> (from <a href="https://zod.dev/">Zod</a>) for their primitive fields.</p>
<div class="flex items-center gap-2 font-bold"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-file-code h-4 w-4"><path d="M10 12.5 8 15l2 2.5"></path><path d="m14 12.5 2 2.5-2 2.5"></path><path d="M14 2v4a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h4"></path><path d="M15 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V7z"></path></svg> <!-- -->schema.ts</div>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { co</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> z } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> TodoProject</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  tasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> ListOfTasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>This gives us schema info that is available for type inference <em>and</em> at runtime.</p>
<p>Check out the inferred type of <code>project</code> in the example below, as well as the input <code>.create()</code> expects.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { Group } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { TodoProject</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> ListOfTasks } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "./schema"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> project</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> TodoProject</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "New Project"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    tasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ListOfTasks</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([]</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Group</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">())</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  Group</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>When creating CoValues that contain other CoValues, you can pass in a plain JSON object.
Jazz will automatically create the CoValues for you.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> group</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Group</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.makePublic</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> publicProject</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> TodoProject</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "New Project"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    tasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> []</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA"> // Permissions are inherited, so the tasks list will also be public</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  group</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<div class="border-l-4 p-4 pl-6 dark:bg-red-200/5 overflow-hidden relative rounded-sm border-blue-400 bg-blue-50 dark:border-blue-500 dark:bg-blue-200/5 flex gap-2 items-center my-4"><span class="text-sm font-bold flex items-center gap-1 text-blue-700 dark:text-blue-400"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="72" height="72" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info rounded-lg text-stone-700 dark:text-stone-100 absolute -z-10 right-0 opacity-5 top-0 rotate-12 pointer-events-none" aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info rounded-xs text-stone-700 dark:text-stone-100" aria-hidden="true"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg></span><span class="text-sm"><p>To learn more about how permissions work when creating nested CoValues with plain JSON objects,
refer to <a href="/docs/react/permissions-and-sharing/cascading-permissions#ownership-on-implicit-covalue-creation">Ownership on implicit CoValue creation</a>.</p></span></div>
<h2 id="types-of-covalues" class="group"><a href="#types-of-covalues" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Types of CoValues</span></h2>
<h3 id="comap-declaration" class="group"><a href="#comap-declaration" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer"><code>CoMap</code> (declaration)</span></h3>
<p>CoMaps are the most commonly used type of CoValue. They are the equivalent of JSON objects (Collaborative editing follows a last-write-wins strategy per-key).</p>
<p>You can either declare struct-like CoMaps:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Task</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  completed</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.boolean</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>Or record-like CoMaps (key-value pairs, where keys are always <code>string</code>):</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ColourToHex</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.record</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ColorToFruit</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.record</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Fruit);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>See the corresponding sections for <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/comaps#creating-comaps">creating</a>,
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/subscription-and-loading">subscribing/loading</a>,
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/comaps#reading-from-comaps">reading from</a> and
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/comaps#updating-comaps">updating</a> CoMaps.</p>
<h3 id="colist-declaration" class="group"><a href="#colist-declaration" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer"><code>CoList</code> (declaration)</span></h3>
<p>CoLists are ordered lists and are the equivalent of JSON arrays. (They support concurrent insertions and deletions, maintaining a consistent order.)</p>
<p>You define them by specifying the type of the items they contain:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ListOfColors</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ListOfTasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Task);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>See the corresponding sections for <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/colists#creating-colists">creating</a>,
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/subscription-and-loading">subscribing/loading</a>,
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/colists#reading-from-colists">reading from</a> and
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/colists#updating-colists">updating</a> CoLists.</p>
<h3 id="cofeed-declaration" class="group"><a href="#cofeed-declaration" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer"><code>CoFeed</code> (declaration)</span></h3>
<p>CoFeeds are a special CoValue type that represent a feed of values for a set of users/sessions (Each session of a user gets its own append-only feed).</p>
<p>They allow easy access of the latest or all items belonging to a user or their sessions. This makes them particularly useful for user presence, reactions, notifications, etc.</p>
<p>You define them by specifying the type of feed item:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> FeedOfTasks</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.feed</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Task);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>See the corresponding sections for <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/overview#creating-cofeeds">creating</a>,
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/subscription-and-loading">subscribing/loading</a>,
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/cofeeds#reading-from-cofeeds">reading from</a> and
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/cofeeds#writing-to-cofeeds">writing to</a> CoFeeds.</p>
<h3 id="filestream-declaration" class="group"><a href="#filestream-declaration" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer"><code>FileStream</code> (declaration)</span></h3>
<p>FileStreams are a special type of CoValue that represent binary data. (They are created by a single user and offer no internal collaboration.)</p>
<p>They allow you to upload and reference files.</p>
<p>You typically don&#x27;t need to declare or extend them yourself, you simply refer to the built-in <code>co.fileStream()</code> from another CoValue:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Document</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  title</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  file</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.fileStream</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>See the corresponding sections for <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/filestreams#creating-filestreams">creating</a>,
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/subscription-and-loading">subscribing/loading</a>,
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/filestreams#reading-from-filestreams">reading from</a> and
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/filestreams#writing-to-filestreams">writing to</a> FileStreams.</p>
<p><strong>Note: For images, we have a special, higher-level <code>co.image()</code> helper, see <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/imagedef">ImageDefinition</a>.</strong></p>
<h3 id="unions-of-comaps-declaration" class="group"><a href="#unions-of-comaps-declaration" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Unions of CoMaps (declaration)</span></h3>
<p>You can declare unions of CoMaps that have discriminating fields, using <code>co.discriminatedUnion()</code>.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ButtonWidget</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  type</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"button"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  label</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> SliderWidget</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  type</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"slider"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  min</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.number</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  max</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.number</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> WidgetUnion</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.discriminatedUnion</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"type"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> [</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  ButtonWidget</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  SliderWidget</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">]);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>See the corresponding sections for <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/schemas/schemaunions#creating-schema-unions">creating</a>,
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/subscription-and-loading">subscribing/loading</a> and
<a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/schemas/schemaunions#narrowing-unions">narrowing</a> schema unions.</p>
<h2 id="covalue-fielditem-types" class="group"><a href="#covalue-fielditem-types" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">CoValue field/item types</span></h2>
<p>Now that we&#x27;ve seen the different types of CoValues, let&#x27;s see more precisely how we declare the fields or items they contain.</p>
<h3 id="primitive-fields" class="group"><a href="#primitive-fields" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Primitive fields</span></h3>
<p>You can declare primitive field types using <code>z</code> (re-exported in <code>jazz-tools</code> from <a href="https://zod.dev/">Zod</a>).</p>
<p>Here&#x27;s a quick overview of the primitive types you can use:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// For simple strings</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.number</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// For numbers</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.boolean</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// For booleans</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// For dates</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.literal</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"waiting"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "ready"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">]); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// For enums</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>Finally, for more complex JSON data, that you <em>don&#x27;t want to be collaborative internally</em> (but only ever update as a whole), you can use more complex Zod types.</p>
<p>For example, you can use <code>z.object()</code> to represent an internally immutable position:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Sprite</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">  // assigned as a whole</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  position</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.object</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({ x</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.number</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> y</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.number</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">() })</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>Or you could use a <code>z.tuple()</code>:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> SpriteWithTuple</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">  // assigned as a whole</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  position</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.tuple</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">([</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.number</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.number</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()])</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="references-to-other-covalues" class="group"><a href="#references-to-other-covalues" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">References to other CoValues</span></h3>
<p>To represent complex structured data with Jazz, you form trees or graphs of CoValues that reference each other.</p>
<p>Internally, this is represented by storing the IDs of the referenced CoValues in the corresponding fields, but Jazz abstracts this away, making it look like nested CoValues you can get or assign/insert.</p>
<p>The important caveat here is that <strong>a referenced CoValue might or might not be loaded yet,</strong> but we&#x27;ll see what exactly that means in <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/subscription-and-loading">Subscribing and Deep Loading</a>.</p>
<p>In Schemas, you declare references by just using the schema of the referenced CoValue:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ListOfPeople</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Person);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Company</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  members</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> ListOfPeople</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="optional-references" class="group"><a href="#optional-references" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Optional References</span></h4>
<p>You can make schema fields optional using either <code>z.optional()</code> or <code>co.optional()</code>, depending on the type of value:</p>
<ul>
<li>Use <code>z.optional()</code> for primitive Zod values like <code>z.string()</code>, <code>z.number()</code>, or <code>z.boolean()</code></li>
<li>Use <code>co.optional()</code> for CoValues like <code>co.map()</code>, <code>co.list()</code>, or <code>co.record()</code></li>
</ul>
<p>You can make references optional with <code>co.optional()</code>:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> PersonWithOptionalProperties</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  age</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.number</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">())</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA"> // primitive</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  pet</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.optional</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Pet)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA"> // CoValue</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="recursive-references" class="group"><a href="#recursive-references" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Recursive References</span></h4>
<p>You can wrap references in getters. This allows you to defer evaluation until the property is accessed. This technique is particularly useful for defining circular references, including recursive (self-referencing) schemas, or mutually recursive schemas.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> SelfReferencingPerson</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  get</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> bestFriend</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    return</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Person;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>You can use the same technique for mutually recursive references:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> MutuallyRecursivePerson</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  name</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  get</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> friends</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">() {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    return</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> ListOfFriends;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ListOfFriends</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.list</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(Person);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>If you try to reference <code>ListOfPeople</code> in <code>Person</code> without using a getter, you&#x27;ll run into a <code>ReferenceError</code> because of the <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Statements/let#temporal_dead_zone_tdz">temporal dead zone</a>.</p>
<h3 id="helper-methods" class="group"><a href="#helper-methods" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Helper methods</span></h3>
<p>If you find yourself repeating the same logic to access computed CoValues properties,
you can define helper functions to encapsulate it for better reusability:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  firstName</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  lastName</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  dateOfBirth</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> z</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> co</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">loaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> Person>;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> function</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> getPersonFullName</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Person</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  return</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> `</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">${</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">person</span><span style="color:#969696;--shiki-dark:#969696">.firstName</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">}</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> ${</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">person</span><span style="color:#969696;--shiki-dark:#969696">.lastName</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">}</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">`</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">function</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> differenceInYears</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(date1</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> date2</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> diffTime</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Math</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.abs</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">date1</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.getTime</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">() </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">-</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> date2</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.getTime</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  return</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Math</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.ceil</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(diffTime </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">/</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">1000</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> *</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 60</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> *</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 60</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> *</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 24</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> *</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 365.25</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">));</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> function</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> getPersonAgeAsOf</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> date</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  return</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> differenceInYears</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(date</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> person</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.dateOfBirth);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> Person</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  firstName</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "John"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  lastName</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Doe"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  dateOfBirth</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> new</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"1990-01-01"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> fullName</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> getPersonFullName</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(person);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> age</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> getPersonAgeAsOf</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> new</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Date</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">());</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>Similarly, you can encapsulate logic needed to update CoValues:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> function</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> updatePersonName</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> fullName</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  const</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> [</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">firstName</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> lastName</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">] </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> fullName</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.split</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">" "</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  person</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"firstName"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> firstName);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  person</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.set</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"lastName"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> lastName);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">person</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.firstName</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> person</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.lastName); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// John Doe</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">updatePersonName</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(person</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "Jane Doe"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">person</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.firstName</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> person</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.lastName); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Jane Doe</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div><div class="flex flex-row justify-start flex-wrap items-center gap-2 py-2"><strong>Was this page helpful?</strong><div><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg text-center w-fit text-nowrap text-sm py-1 px-2 bg-white dark:bg-black hover:bg-stone-100/50
